        name: 'LIVE Кубок Первого канала по хоккею',
        src: 'https://www.1tv.ru/iframed/eump-embedlive_yo.html?channel_id=1&channels_api_url=https://api.1tv.ru/v2/special/channels.json'
      },
      player_container = $('.player__container__middle'),
      player_embed = $('.embedlive-remote', player_container),
      air = {
        name: 'Телеэфир',
        src: player_embed.prop('src')
      },
      schedule_container = $('@schedule'),
      broadcast_buttons = false,

      broadcast_timer = setInterval(function() {
        check_broadcast_timer();
      }, 2000);


    $(player_container).on('click', '.button', function(){

      if(!$(this).hasClass('button_active')) {
        var src = $(this).data('src');
        $('.button', player_container).removeClass('button_active');
        $(this).addClass('button_active');
        if ($(this).hasClass('button_air')) {
          schedule_container.fadeIn('slow', change_stream_src(air.src));
        }
        else {
          air.src = player_embed.prop('src');
          schedule_container.fadeOut('slow', change_stream_src(src));
        }
      }
    });

    function check_broadcast_timer() {
      if (broadcast.time_start < window.one_tv_user_settings.time &&
        broadcast.time_end > window.one_tv_user_settings.time)
      {
        add_broadcast_buttons();
      }
      else {
        remove_broadcast_buttons();
      }
        }

        function insert_after(elementInstertAfter, parentElement) {
            return parentElement.parentNode.insertBefore(elementInstertAfter, parentElement.nextSibling);
        }

        function add_all_broadcast_block() {
            var page = document.querySelector('.live');
            var beforeElement = page.querySelector('.schedule__banner');
            var afterElement = document.createElement('div');

            afterElement.innerHTML = "<div class='live-broadcasts'>" +
                "<div class='live-broadcasts__title-wrapper'>" +
                "<div class='live-broadcasts__title text-sm-center'>" +
                "Все эфиры и онлайн-трансляции Первого канала" +
                "</div>" +
				  
                "</div>" +
                "<div class='live-broadcasts__wrapper'>" +
                "<div class='container live-broadcasts__container'>" +
                    "<div class='row' style='justify-content: center'>" +
                    "<div class='col-sm-6 col-lg-6'>" +
                        "<a class='live-broadcasts__card' href='/sport'>" +
                        "<div class='live-broadcasts__card-wrapper'>" +
                            "<div class='live-broadcasts__card-wrapper-inner'>" +
                            "<div class='live-broadcasts__picture'>" +
                                "<img src='https://static.1tv.ru/uploads/photo/image/2020/12/17/12484/big/12484_big_b349235de3.jpg'>" +
                            "</div>" +
                            "<div class='live-broadcasts__description__wrapper' style='background-image: linear-gradient(180deg, #00000000 30%, #4c6897 80%); color: #fff'>" +
                                "<div style='padding: 0 10px'class='live-broadcasts__description'>" +
                                "<div class='live-broadcasts__channel'>" +
                                    "<svg width='28' height='19' viewBox='0 0 28 19' fill='none' xmlns='http://www.w3.org/2000/svg'>" +
                                    "<path fill-rule='evenodd' clip-rule='evenodd' d='M0.722168 7.07693L1.40365 4.66981L15.3253 0L10.7497 16.3684L5.49254 17.8127L9.28936 4.18838L0.722168 7.07693ZM1.98796 18.7755L5.44405 6.25849L8.16997 5.34378L4.61654 18.0534L1.98796 18.7755Z' fill='#5E16CE'></path> " +
                                    "<line x1='26.7586' y1='0.137361' x2='21.5432' y2='18.3913' stroke='#5E16CE'></line> " +
                                    "</svg>" +
                                    "live" +
                                "</div>" +
                                "<p> Кубок Первого канала по хоккею<br>" +
                                "</p>" +
                                "</div>" +
                                "<div class='button button_play' style='color: #fff; border-color: #fff'>" +
                                "Смотреть онлайн" +
                                "</div>" +
                            "</div>" +
                            "</div>" +
                        "</div>" +
                        "</a>" +
                    "</div>" +
                    "</div>" +
                "</div>" +
			  
                "</div>" +
            "</div>"
            insert_after(afterElement, beforeElement);
        }

    function add_broadcast_buttons() {
      if (broadcast_buttons === true) return;
      player_container.prepend($(
        "<div class='broadcasts'>" +
          "<a class='button button_active button_air' data-src='" + air.src + "'>" + air.name + "</a>" +
          "<a class='button' data-src='" + broadcast.src + "'>" + broadcast.name + "</a>" +
        "</div>"));
            broadcast_buttons = true;

            add_all_broadcast_block()
    }

    function remove_broadcast_buttons() {
      if (broadcast_buttons === false) return;
      $('.broadcasts', player_container).remove();
      broadcast_buttons = false;
      change_stream_src(air.src);						 
    }

    function change_stream_src(src) {
      player_embed.prop('src', src);
    }
  }
});
</script>

   <script>
    $(document).on('start_live_mini_player', function(){
    var path = window.location.pathname || ''
    if ((path === '/' || path.substr(0, 10) === '/schedule/') && window.matchMedia('(min-width: 733px)').matches && !EUMP.device.is('mobile') && !EUMP.device.is('smarttv') && ['IE', 'Edge'].indexOf(EUMP.device.param('browser.name')) == -1) {
      if (window.location.hostname !== 'free.1tv.ru') mainMiniPlayer.init();
    }
  });
  var mainMiniPlayer = {
    state: {},
    load_state: function () {
      try {
        mainMiniPlayer.state = JSON.parse(localStorage.getItem('mainPageMiniPlayer') || '{}');
      } catch (e) {
        mainMiniPlayer.state = {};
      }
      return mainMiniPlayer.state;
    },
    save_state: function () {
      try {
        localStorage.setItem('mainPageMiniPlayer', JSON.stringify(mainMiniPlayer.state));
      } catch (e) { }
    },
    init: function () {
      var head = document.getElementsByTagName('head')[0];
      var link = document.createElement('link');
      link.id = 'mini-player';
      link.rel = 'stylesheet';
      link.type = 'text/css';
      link.href = '//static.1tv.ru/player/eump-branded/1tv/miniplayer/versions/v1.1.5/miniplayer.css';
      link.media = 'all';
      head.appendChild(link);

      var s = document.createElement('script');
      s.setAttribute('src', '//static.1tv.ru/player/eump-branded/1tv/miniplayer/versions/v1.1.5/miniplayer.js');

      s.onload = function () {
        $('main').append($('#js-main-video'));
        setTimeout(function () {
          mainMiniPlayer.load_state();
          if (EUMP.device.api('page').visible()) {
            mainMiniPlayer.initPlayer();
          } else {
            EUMP.fw.window.bind('pagevisibilitychange', mainMiniPlayer.initPlayer, true, false);
          }
        }, window.MINI_PLAYER_APPEAR_DELAY);
      };
      document.body.appendChild(s);

    },
    initPlayer: function () {
      if (mainMiniPlayer.state.muted == false && Date.parse(mainMiniPlayer.state.muteTimestamp) > Date.now() - 1000 * 3600 * 24) {
        mainMiniPlayer.state.muteTimestamp = String(new Date());
        mainMiniPlayer.save_state();
      } else {
        mainMiniPlayer.state.muted = true;
        mainMiniPlayer.state.muteTimestamp = '';
      }
      var start = EUMP.global.getActivePlayer() ? 'none' : 'auto';
      var miniPlayerConfig = {
        muted: true,
        start: start,
        openLinkInNewWindow: false,
        onVolumeChange: function (e) {
          mainMiniPlayer.state.muted = e.muted;
          if (mainMiniPlayer.state.muted === false) {
            mainMiniPlayer.state.muteTimestamp = String(new Date());
          }
          mainMiniPlayer.save_state();
        }
      };
      var orbitPlus4Enabled = Cookies.get('player_id') === "orbit_3";
      if (orbitPlus4Enabled) {
        var orbitPlus4Config = {
          starterOpts: {
            playerOpts: {
              liveTimeOffset: -25200,
              pluginsOpts: {
                stat1tv: {
                  rt_stat: {
                    channel: "1tvmini-orbit-plus-4"
                  },
                }
              }
            }
          },
          api: {
            sources: {
              url: "//stream.1tv.ru/api/playlist/1tv-orbit-plus-4_as_array.json?r=[random]",
              type: "json"
            },
            restrictions: {
              url: "//stream.1tv.ru/api/restrictions_orb3.json?r=[random]",
              type: "json"
            },
            schedule: {
              url: "//stream.1tv.ru/api/schedule3.json?r=[random]",
              type: "json"
            },
            protectionKey: {
              type: "api"
            }
          }
        };
        window.EUMP.fw.extend(miniPlayerConfig, orbitPlus4Config);
      }
      createMiniPlayer('#js-main-video-eump', miniPlayerConfig)
        .then(function (player) {
          $('#js-main-video').removeClass('hidden');
          $('.js-main-video-preview-title').on('click', function () {
            player.open();
          });
          $('#js-main-video .main-video-preview-close').on('click', function () {
            $('#js-main-video').addClass('hidden');
            player.pause();
            mainMiniPlayer.save_state();
          }.bind(this));
        }.bind(this))
        .catch(function (e) {
        });
    }
  }
   </script>
